            "**ì§ˆë¬¸34 : ì‹œê°í™” ë‹¨ê³„ ì‹œì‘**  \n**ë‹µë³€34 : ì—ì¿¼í‹°ì»¤ë¸Œ ê·¸ë¦¬ê¸° ê°€ì´ë“œ**\n\n---\n\n# 1) ê°œìš”\n- ëª©í‘œ: **ë°±í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ê²°ê³¼(ì†ìµ/ìì‚° ê³¡ì„ )**ë¥¼ `matplotlib`ìœ¼ë¡œ ê·¸ë¦¼ íŒŒì¼ë¡œ ì €ì¥  \n- ì‚°ì¶œë¬¼: `reports/equity_curve.png` (í•„ìˆ˜), `reports/equity_curve.svg` (ì„ íƒ)  \n- ì „ì œ: 1~33ë‹¨ê³„ê¹Œì§€ì˜ êµ¬ì¡°ì™€ ì‹¤í–‰ íë¦„ ìœ ì§€(í”„ë¡œì íŠ¸/ê°€ìƒí™˜ê²½/ëª¨ë“ˆ êµ¬ì¡°) îˆ€fileciteîˆ‚turn0file0îˆ\n\n---\n\n# 2) í´ë” ì¤€ë¹„\ní„°ë¯¸ë„(í”„ë¡œì íŠ¸ ë£¨íŠ¸)ì—ì„œ:\n```bash\n# (Windows PowerShell) í”„ë¡œì íŠ¸ ë£¨íŠ¸ì—ì„œ ì‹¤í–‰\nmkdir reports\n```\n> ì´ë¯¸ ìˆìœ¼ë©´ ë„˜ì–´ê°€ë©´ ë©ë‹ˆë‹¤. (ì—†ìœ¼ë©´ ì €ì¥ ì‹œ ì—ëŸ¬)\n\n---\n\n# 3) ì‹œê°í™” ìœ í‹¸ ì¶”ê°€ (ìƒˆ íŒŒì¼)\n`src/visualize.py` ìƒì„± í›„ ì•„ë˜ ì½”ë“œ ì „ì²´ ë¶™ì—¬ë„£ê¸°:\n\n```python\n# src/visualize.py\nfrom __future__ import annotations\nimport os\nimport matplotlib\nmatplotlib.use(\"Agg\")  # GUI ì—†ì´ íŒŒì¼ë¡œ ì €ì¥\nimport matplotlib.pyplot as plt\nimport pandas as pd\n\ndef ensure_dir(path: str) -> None:\n    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(path), exist_ok=True)\n\ndef _pick_equity_series(df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"\n    ê°€ëŠ¥í•œ ì»¬ëŸ¼ ìš°ì„ ìˆœìœ„ë¡œ ì—ì¿¼í‹° ì‹œë¦¬ì¦ˆë¥¼ ì¶”ì¶œí•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.\n    1) 'equity' (ì ˆëŒ€ìì‚°ê³¡ì„ ) \n    2) 'cum_pnl' (ëˆ„ì ì†ìµì´ ìˆëŠ” ê²½ìš° ì´ˆê¸°ìë³¸ ê°€ì •)\n    3) 'strategy_return' ë˜ëŠ” 'return' ëˆ„ì ê³±(1+r)ë¡œ ë³€í™˜\n    ë§ˆì§€ë§‰ìœ¼ë¡œ price ê¸°ì¤€ì˜ buy&hold ëˆ„ì ìˆ˜ìµë¥ ì„ ë°±ì—…ìœ¼ë¡œ ì‚¬ìš©.\n    \"\"\"\n    candidates = [c for c in df.columns]\n    # ì ˆëŒ€ ì—ì¿¼í‹°ê°€ ì´ë¯¸ ìˆëŠ” ê²½ìš°\n    if 'equity' in candidates:\n        s = df['equity'].astype(float)\n        s.name = 'equity'\n        return s\n\n    # ëˆ„ì  ì†ìµë§Œ ìˆëŠ” ê²½ìš°: ì´ˆê¸°ìë³¸ 1.0 ê°€ì •í•˜ì—¬ equity ë³€í™˜\n    if 'cum_pnl' in candidates:\n        s = 1.0 + df['cum_pnl'].astype(float)\n        s.name = 'equity'\n        return s\n\n    # ìˆ˜ìµë¥ ì´ ìˆëŠ” ê²½ìš°\n    for rcol in ('strategy_return', 'return', 'ret'):\n        if rcol in candidates:\n            s = (1.0 + df[rcol].astype(float)).cumprod()\n            s.name = 'equity'\n            return s\n\n    # ì•„ë¬´ê²ƒë„ ì—†ìœ¼ë©´ ê°€ê²©ì˜ buy&hold ê¸°ì¤€ìœ¼ë¡œë¼ë„ í‘œì‹œ\n    for pcol in ('close', 'price', 'adj_close'):\n        if pcol in candidates:\n            px = df[pcol].astype(float)\n            base = px.iloc[0] if len(px) else 1.0\n            s = px / base\n            s.name = 'equity'\n            return s\n\n    # ë§ˆì§€ë§‰ ë°±ì—…: ì „ë¶€ ì‹¤íŒ¨ ì‹œ ë‹¨ì¡°ì¦ê°€ ë”ë¯¸\n    s = pd.Series(range(1, len(df) + 1), index=df.index, name='equity').astype(float)\n    return s / float(max(1, len(df)))\n\ndef plot_equity_curve(df: pd.DataFrame, out_png: str, out_svg: str | None = None,\n                      title: str = \"Equity Curve\") -> str:\n    \"\"\"\n    dfì—ì„œ ì—ì¿¼í‹° ê³¡ì„ ì„ ê³„ì‚°/ì„ íƒí•˜ì—¬ ì €ì¥.\n    ë°˜í™˜: ì €ì¥ëœ PNG ê²½ë¡œ\n    \"\"\"\n    ensure_dir(out_png)\n    equity = _pick_equity_series(df)\n    x = df.index if not isinstance(df.index, pd.RangeIndex) else df.get('date', None)\n    # x ì¶•: date ì»¬ëŸ¼ì´ ìˆìœ¼ë©´ ì‚¬ìš©, ì—†ìœ¼ë©´ ì¸ë±ìŠ¤\n    if isinstance(x, pd.Series):\n        x = pd.to_datetime(x, errors='coerce')\n\n    plt.figure(figsize=(10, 5))\n    plt.plot(x if x is not None else equity.index, equity, linewidth=1.5)\n    plt.title(title)\n    plt.xlabel(\"Date\" if x is not None else \"Index\")\n    plt.ylabel(\"Equity (normalized)\")\n    plt.grid(True, linestyle='--', alpha=0.4)\n    plt.tight_layout()\n    plt.savefig(out_png, dpi=150)\n    plt.close()\n\n    if out_svg:\n        ensure_dir(out_svg)\n        plt.figure(figsize=(10, 5))\n        plt.plot(x if x is not None else equity.index, equity, linewidth=1.5)\n        plt.title(title)\n        plt.xlabel(\"Date\" if x is not None else \"Index\")\n        plt.ylabel(\"Equity (normalized)\")\n        plt.grid(True, linestyle='--', alpha=0.4)\n        plt.tight_layout()\n        plt.savefig(out_svg)\n        plt.close()\n\n    return out_png\n```\n\n---\n\n# 4) ë©”ì¸ ì‹¤í–‰ íë¦„ì— ì‹œê°í™” ì—°ê²°\n`src/main.py`ì˜ **ëë¶€ë¶„**(ë°±í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰ì´ ëë‚˜ê³  ê²°ê³¼ `df`ë¥¼ ê°–ê³  ìˆëŠ” ì§€ì ) ì•„ë˜ì²˜ëŸ¼ ìˆ˜ì •/ì¶”ê°€:\n\n```python\n# src/main.py (ë°œì·Œ: ë§ˆì§€ë§‰ ë¶€ë¶„ ì˜ˆì‹œ)\n# ... ê¸°ì¡´: ë°ì´í„° ë¡œë“œ -> ì „ëµ ì ìš© -> ë°±í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ -> ê²°ê³¼ df ìƒì„±\n\nfrom visualize import plot_equity_curve\nimport os\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    # ì˜ˆ: backtest(df_prices, fast=..., slow=...) ë“±ì˜ ê²°ê³¼ë¥¼ df_resultë¡œ ë°›ì•˜ë‹¤ê³  ê°€ì •\n    # df_result = backtest(...)\n    # df_resultëŠ” ìµœì†Œí•œ ë‚ ì§œ/ê°€ê²©/ìˆ˜ìµë¥ /ëˆ„ì ì†ìµ/ì—ì¿¼í‹° ì¤‘ í•˜ë‚˜ê°€ ìˆì–´ì•¼ í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.\n\n    reports_dir = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), \"..\", \"reports\")\n    out_png =                    title=\"Equity Curve â€“ AutoTraderAgent\")\n    print(f\"[OK] Equity curve saved to: {os.path.abspath(saved)}\")\n```\n\n> âœ… `df_result` ì´ë¦„ì€ í”„ë¡œì íŠ¸ì—ì„œ ì‚¬ìš© ì¤‘ì¸ ì•„ë˜ ë³´ê°•:\n\n```python\n# visualize.py ì— ì¶”ê°€ (ê°„ë‹¨ í™•ì¥)\ndef plot_equity_vs_bh(df, out_png: str, title: str = \"Strategy vs Buy&Hold\"):\n    import pandas as pd\n    import matplotlib.pyplot as plt\n    eq = _pick_equity_series(df)\n    # Buy&Hold\n    px_col = None\n    for p in ('close', 'price', 'adj_close'):\n        if p in df.columns:\n            px_col = p\n            break\n    if px_col is not None:\n        bh = df[px_col].astype(float) / float(df[px_col].iloc[0])\n    else:\n        bh = None\n\n    x = df.get('date', None)\n    if isinstance(x, pd.Series):\n        x = pd.to_datetime(x, errors='coerce')\n\n    plt.figure(figsize=(10,5))\n    if bh is not None:\n        plt.plot(x if x is not None else bh.index, bh, label=\"Buy & Hold\", linewidth=1.2)\n    plt.plot(x if x is not None else eq.index, eq, label=\"Strategy\", linewidth=1.6)\n    plt.title(title)\n    plt.xlabel(\"Date\" if x is not None else \"Index\")\n    plt.ylabel(\"Equity (normalized)\")\n    plt.grid(True, linestyle='--', alpha=0.4)\n    plt.legend()\n    plt.tight_layout()\n    plt.savefig(out_png, dpi=150)\n    plt.close()\n```\n\n`main.py`ì—ì„œ:\n```python\nfrom visualize import plot_equity_curve, plot_equity_vs_bh\n# ...\nout_cmp = os.path.join(reports_dir, \"equity_vs_bh.png\")\nplot_equity_vs_bh(df_result, out_png=out_cmp, title=\"Strategy vs Buy&Hold\")\n```\n\n---\n\n# 8) ë‹¤ìŒ ë‹¨ê³„ ì˜ˆê³  (ìë™ ìµœì í™”/ë©€í‹°ìì‚°/ë¡œê·¸)\n- **ì§ˆë¬¸35(ì˜ˆì •)**: (ë³µë¶™ ê°€ëŠ¥)\n\n### â‘  `reports/` í´ë” ë§Œë“¤ê¸°\nPowerShell(í”„ë¡œì íŠ¸ ë£¨íŠ¸)ì—ì„œ:\n```powershell\nmkdir reports\n```\n\n### â‘¡ ì‹œê°í™” ìœ í‹¸ íŒŒì¼ ìƒì„±: `src/visualize.py`\nì•„ë˜ ìµœì†Œ ë²„ì „ ë¶™ì—¬ë„£ê¸°(íŒŒì¼ í†µì§¸ë¡œ ìƒì„±):\n\n```python\n# src/visualize.py\nfrom __future__ import annotations\nimport os\nimport matplotlib\nmatplotlib.use(\"Agg\")  # GUI ì—†ì´ ì €ì¥ìš©\nimport matplotlib.pyplot as plt\nimport pandas as pd\n\ndef ensure_dir(path: str) -> None:\n    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(path), exist_ok=True)\n\ndef _pick_equity_series(df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.Series:\n    if 'equity' in df.columns:\n        s = df['equity'].astype(float)\n    elif 'cum_pnl' in df.columns:\n        s = 1.0 + df['cum_pnl'].astype(float)\n    elif any(c in df.columns for c in ('strategy_return','return','ret')):\n        c = next(c for c in ('strategy_return','return','ret') if c in df.columns)\n        s = (1.0 + df[c].astype(float)).cumprod()\n    elif any(p in df.columns for p in ('close','price','adj_close')):\n        p = next(p for p in ('close','price','adj_close') if p in df.columns)\n        base = float(df[p].iloc[0])\n        s = df[p].astype(float) / (base if base else 1.0)\n    else:\n        s = pd.Series(range(1, len(df)+1), index=df.index, dtype=float) / max(1, len(df))\n    s.name = 'equity'\n    return s\n\ndef plot_equity_curve(df: pd.DataFrame, out_png: str, out_svg: str|None=None,\n                      title: str=\"Equity Curve\") -> str:\n    ensure_dir(out_png)\n    eq = _pick_equity_series(df)\n    x = df['date'] if 'date' in df.columns else None\n    if isinstance(x, pd.Series):\n        x = pd.to_datetime(x, errors='coerce')\n\n    plt.figure(figsize=(10,5))\n    plt.plot(x if x is not None else eq.index, eq, linewidth=1.5)\n    plt.title(title)\n    plt.xlabel(\"Date\" if x is not None else \"Index\")\n    plt.ylabel(\"Equity (normalized)\")\n    plt.grid(True, linestyle='--', alpha=0.4)\n    plt.tight_layout()\n    plt.savefig(out_png, dpi=150)\n    plt.close()\n\n    if out_svg:\n        ensure_dir(out_svg)\n        plt.figure(figsize=(10,5))\n        plt.plot(x if x is not None else eq.index, eq, linewidth=1.5)\n        plt.title(title)\n        plt.xlabel(\"Date\" if x is not None else \"Index\")\n        plt.ylabel(\"Equity (normalized)\")\n        plt.grid(True, linestyle='--', alpha=0.4)\n        plt.tight_layout()\n        plt.savefig(out_svg)\n        plt.close()\n    return out_png\n```\n\n### â‘¢ ë©”ì¸ì— ì—°ê²°: `src/main.py` ë§ˆì§€ë§‰ ë¶€ë¶„ ì¶”ê°€\n> ì£¼ì˜: `df_result`ëŠ” ë‹¹ì‹ ì˜ ë°±í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ê²°ê³¼ ë°ì´í„°í”„ë ˆì„ ë³€ìˆ˜ëª…ìœ¼ë¡œ ë°”ê¿”ë„ ë©ë‹ˆë‹¤.\n\n```python\n# src/main.py (ë§ë¯¸ì— ì¶”ê°€)\nfrom visualize import plot_equity_curve\nimport os\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    # ... ì•ì—ì„œ df_result ìƒì„± ì™„ë£Œ ê°€ì •\n    reports_dir = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), \"..\", \"reports\")\n    out_png = os.path.join(reports_dir, \"equity_curve.png\")\n    out_svg = os.path.join(reports_dir, \"equity_curve.svg\")\n\n    saved = plot_equity_curve(\n        df_result,\n        out_png=out_png,\n        out_svg=out_svg,\n        title=\"Equity Curve â€“ AutoTraderAgent\"\n    )\n    print(f\"[OK] Equity curve saved to: {os.path.abspath(saved)}\")\n```\n\n### â‘£ ì‹¤í–‰\n```powershell\n# ê°€ìƒí™˜ê²½
